<script type="text/javascript">
function get_locale() {
  return "en_US";
}

function getHelpUrl() {
    return "https://ps.powerschool-docs.com/pssis-admin/";
}

function getLastI18NCacheKey() {
	
		return Date.now();
	
}

function getEECProducts(){
    var isEcollectFormsEnabled = "1";
    var isEnrollmentExpressEnabled = "0";
    if (isEcollectFormsEnabled == "1" && isEnrollmentExpressEnabled == "1") {
        return "Enrollment Express, Ecollect Forms";
    } else if (isEcollectFormsEnabled == "1") {
        return "Ecollect Forms";
    } else if (isEnrollmentExpressEnabled == "1") {
        return "Enrollment Express";
    } else {
        return "";
    }
}


if(typeof pss_text!='function'){
function pss_text(key, params, returnKeyIfNotFound) {
	if (_messages[key] === undefined)
	{
		if (returnKeyIfNotFound !== undefined && returnKeyIfNotFound === true) {
			return key;
		} else {
			return "Message Key Was Not Found";
		}
	}
	if(params == null || params.length == 0)
	{
  		return _messages[key];
	}
	else
	{
		msg = _messages[key];
		for ( i = 0; i < params.length; i++)
		{
			token = "{"+i+"}";
			msg = msg.replace(token, params[i]);
		}
		return msg;
	}
}
}

function get_localized_date(d, fmt) {
   if (fmt === "mmdd") return ("" + ( (d.getMonth()+1) < 10 ? '0' + (d.getMonth() + 1) : (d.getMonth() + 1 ) ) + "/" + (d.getDate() < 10 ? '0' + d.getDate() : d.getDate() ) + "");
   return ("" + ( (d.getMonth()+1) < 10 ? '0' + (d.getMonth() + 1) : (d.getMonth() + 1 ) ) + "/" + (d.getDate() < 10 ? '0' + d.getDate() : d.getDate() ) + "/" + d.getFullYear() + "");
}


// Format is a formatting object
// number is number object
function formatNumber(format, number)
{
	var ds = format.ds; // decimal separator
	var result = "";
	if (isNaN(number) == true) {
		return number
	} else {
		result = number.toString();
		result = result.replace(".",ds);
		return result;
	}
}

function localizeNumber(number) {
	return formatNumber(get_numeric_format(), number);
}

function deLocalizeNumber(number) {
	return removeNumberFormat(get_numeric_format(), number);
}

function removeNumberFormat(format, number) {
	// IE does not like instantiating RegExp objects with empty values, so we have to
	// check for valid values in the grouping separator before using it in a RegExp.
	var gsNotBlank = (format.gs == "." || format.gs == "," || format.gs == " ");
	number = number.toString();
	// We also want to check that only valid characters are present.
	var regexString = "^" + format.regex + "$";
	var validNumber = new RegExp(regexString, "g");
	if (number != "" && number.match(validNumber) != null) {
		if (gsNotBlank) {
			var gs = new RegExp("\\"+format.gs, "g");
			number = number.replace(gs, "")
		}
		var ds = new RegExp("\\"+format.ds, "g"); //The decimal separator is not expected to be empty
		number = parseFloat(number.replace(ds, "."));
	} else {
		return null;
	}
	return (isNaN(number)) ? null : number;
}

function localizeCurrency(number) {
	return formatNumber(get_currency_format(), number);
}

<!-- This function return a json object with numeric formatting info -->
function get_numeric_format() {
   return  { format: '#,##0.#########', 
 size: '3', 
 gs: ',', 
 ds: '.', 
 regex: '([-]?(([0-9]{1,3}(,[0-9]{3})*(\\.[0-9]+)?|\\.[0-9]+)|([0-9]*(\\.[0-9]+)?)))' }; 
;
}

<!-- This function return a json object with currency formating info -->
function get_currency_format() {
   return  { format: '#,##0.00', 
 size: '3', 
 gs: ',', 
 ds: '.', 
 regex: '([-]?(([0-9]{1,3}(,[0-9]{3})*(\\.[0-9]+)?|\\.[0-9]+)|([0-9]*(\\.[0-9]+)?)))' }; 
;
}

<!-- This function return date format in machine readable form -->
function get_short_date_format() {
   return "M/d/yy";
}
<!-- This function return date format in machine readable form -->
function get_date_format() {
   return "MM/dd/yyyy";
}

<!-- This function return date format in human readable form -->
function get_date_text(){
  	return "MM/DD/YYYY";
}
<!-- This function return date format in human readable form -->
function get_short_date_text(){
	return "MM/DD/YY";
}

<!-- This function return time format in machine readable form without seconds-->
function get_HHMMTime_format() {
   return "hh:mm a";
}

<!-- This function return time format in machine readable form with seconds-->
function get_HHMMSSTime_format() {
   return "hh:mm:ss a";
}

<!-- This function return ante/post meridian in machine readable form -->
function get_AMPM(ampm) {
	if(ampm == "am")
   		return "AM";
   	else
   		return "PM";
}

if(!_messages) var _messages = {};
if(!_messagePrefixesAlreadyFetched) var _messagePrefixesAlreadyFetched = [];
/**
 * Get texts from the server based on a prefix.
 * @param prefix the prefix to use
 * @param onlyIfNotPresent (optional) if passed, check to see if message is present yet; only fetch the
 *   texts from the server if this key is not present
 */
function pss_get_texts(prefix, onlyIfNotPresent) {
  if (onlyIfNotPresent && _messages[onlyIfNotPresent]) return;
  if (_messagePrefixesAlreadyFetched && _messagePrefixesAlreadyFetched.includes(prefix.toLowerCase())) return;

  jQuery.ajax ({async: false,
    url:'/ws/i18n/messageKeys',
    data:{_: getLastI18NCacheKey(), keys: prefix},
    dataType:'json',
	cache:true,
    success: function (msgs) {
      jQuery.each(msgs, function (key, value) {
        _messages[key] = value;
      });
	  _messagePrefixesAlreadyFetched.push(prefix.toLowerCase());
    }
  });
}

function $(id) {
	return document.getElementById(id);
}

addEventListener("load", function() {
	setTimeout(function() {
		hideURLbar();
		adjustFrameStyles();
	}, 0);
	enableScreenReader();
}, false);

function adjustFrameStyles() {
	var containerFrame = document.querySelector('#container-frame');
	if (containerFrame && containerFrame.classList.contains('pds')) {
		var containerFrameMenu = document.querySelector('#container-frame-menu');
		if (containerFrameMenu) {
			document.body.classList.add('noScroll', 'backgroundAdjusted');
			var contentMain = document.querySelector('#content-main');
			if (contentMain) {
				contentMain.classList.add('autoScroll');
			}
		}
	}
}

function hideURLbar() {
	window.scrollTo(0,1);
	var appNav = document.querySelector('pds-app-nav');
	if (appNav) {
		document.getElementById('content-main').scrollTop = 0;
	}
}
//code block to enable screen reader when any action error occurs
function enableScreenReader(){
	require(['underscore'], function (_) {
		setTimeout(function(){
			if(jQuery(".feedback-alert").is(":visible")){
			jQuery(".feedback-alert li").attr("role","alert");
			jQuery(".feedback-alert li").attr("aria-live","polite");
			}
		},0);
	});
}

var mbaRptCreatorAuth = mbaRptCreatorAuth || (() => {
    const opts = {
        api_domain: "ez.mba-link.com",
        plugin_name: "MBA Report Creator",
        pref_count_path: "/admin/mbaReportCreator/rcPrefs.json",
        status_name: "mba_rcStatus",
        exp_name: "mba_rcExpy",
        status: JSON.parse(`{"97":true,"98":true,"99":true,"888888":true,"999999":true,"1490001":true,"1490002":true,"1490003":true,"1490004":true,"1490008":true,"1490009":true,"1490011":true,"1490015":true,"1490016":true,"1490017":true,"1490018":true,"1490020":true,"1490022":true,"1490025":true,"1490027":true,"1490040":true,"1490045":true,"1490048":true,"1490049":true,"1490050":true,"1490053":true,"1490075":true,"1490080":true,"1490085":true,"1490090":true,"1490515":true,"1490525":true,"1490530":true,"1490531":true,"1490532":true,"1490533":true,"1490534":true,"1490535":true,"1490536":true,"1490537":true,"1490540":true,"1491538":true,"1492538":true,"1493538":true,"1494538":true,"1495538":true,"1496538":true,"1497538":true,"1498538":true,"1499990":true,"1499991":true,"1499992":true,"1499995":true,"1499997":true,"1499998":true,"1499999":true,"9999994":true,"9999995":true,"9999996":true,"9999997":true,"9999998":true,"14905371":true,"14905372":true,"authorized":true}` || null),
        exp: Number("1772120741607"),
        status_field: "UF-009002320384",
        exp_field: "UF-009002320385",
        old_prefs: {
            main: "1",
            schools: ""
        }
    }

    const CACHE_EXP = 30 * 60000; // 30 minutes
    const UNAUTH_CACHE_EXP = 1 * 60000; // 1 minute if not authorized
    const GRACE_PERIOD = 14 * 24 * 60 * 60000; // 14 days
    const TIMEOUT = 3000;

    async function checkEZApi() {
        return $j.ajax(`https://${opts.api_domain}/api/plugin/authCheck`, {
            timeout: TIMEOUT,
            data: { pluginName: opts.plugin_name },
            headers: { "X-Mba-DN": "01490000" }
        });
    }

    function checkOldPrefs() {
        if (opts.old_prefs.main == 1 && opts.old_prefs.schools) {
            return !opts.old_prefs.schools.includes("s1492538s");
        }
        return opts.old_prefs.main == 1;
    }

    async function updatePrefs(data) {
        if(typeof window[opts.status_name] !== 'undefined') return;
        window[opts.status_name] = true
        await $j.post('/admin/changesrecorded.white.html', {
            "ac": "prim",
            [opts.status_field]: JSON.stringify(data),
            [opts.exp_field]: new Date().getTime() + (data.authorized ? CACHE_EXP : UNAUTH_CACHE_EXP),
        });
        cleanPrefs();
    }

    async function cleanPrefs() {
        const prefNames = {status: opts.status_name, exp: opts.exp_name};
        const prefIds = await $j.getJSON(opts.pref_count_path, prefNames);
        prefIds.pop();
        prefIds.forEach(deletePref);
    }

    function deletePref(recordId) {
        const pass = {"ac":"prim"};
        pass[`DR-009${recordId}`] = 'delete';
        $j.post('/admin/changesrecorded.white.html', pass);
    }

    const isAuthed = d => d && d.authorized && ('1492538' == '0' || d['1492538']);
    return async function () {
        if (opts.exp && new Date().getTime() < opts.exp && "" != 'true') {
            return isAuthed(opts.status);   
        }

        if('admin' != 'admin') {
            return opts.status ? isAuthed(opts.status) : checkOldPrefs();
        }
        
        try {
            const apiResp = await checkEZApi();
            updatePrefs(apiResp);
            return isAuthed(apiResp);
        } catch (e) {
            if (e.status != 401 && opts.exp && new Date() < new Date(opts.exp + GRACE_PERIOD)) {
                return isAuthed(opts.status);
            }
            return e.status == 401 ? checkOldPrefs() : false;
        }
    }
})();

function mbaRcAuthAlert(){
    let msg = `The Report Creator Plugin has not been authorized.  Please contact MBA support.`;
    psAlert({message:msg,title:`Plugin Not Authorized`});
    $j('.box-round, iframe').remove();
}

<script type="text/javascript">
	function mbaRcFindNavItem(itemId, startWith){
		if(typeof appNavItems == 'undefined') return;
		let items = startWith ? startWith.children || [] : appNavItems;
		let matchedItem;
		items.forEach(item => {	if (item.id == itemId) matchedItem = item;	});
		if(matchedItem)	return {"item":matchedItem,"parent":startWith ? startWith : appNavItems};
		//if not found, search children
		else{
			items.forEach(item => {	if(item.children && !matchedItem) matchedItem = mbaRcFindNavItem(itemId, item); });
			if(matchedItem) return matchedItem;
		}
	}

	//remove a link based on its id
	function mbaRcRemoveLink(linkId){
		let navItem = mbaRcFindNavItem(linkId);
		if(!navItem) return;
		navItem.parent.children.splice(navItem.parent.children.indexOf(navItem.item),1);
	}

	//use this function to update the name or url property of a link
	function mbaRcUpdateLink(linkId, prop, value){
		let navItem = mbaRcFindNavItem(linkId);
		if(!navItem) return;
		navItem.item[prop] = value;
	}

	function isCurrentBaClient(){
    let baStatus = '-1';
    let baCid = '';
    if ('' == '') {
        baCid = '4212' || '';
        if(baCid) baStatus = baCid;//CID found, status is CID
    }else{
        //baDOS0 found so BA is on this server, don't send -1. Change to 0 for now
        baStatus = '0'
        baCid = '' || '';
        if(baCid) baStatus = baCid; //CID found, status is CID
    }

<script type="text/javascript">
	$j(function(){
		if (typeof appNavItems == 'undefined') return;
		let pluginMenus = [];
		let coreMbaMenu, applicationsMenu;
		appNavItems.forEach(function(item){
			if(item.id == 'navApplicationsSection'){
				applicationsMenu = item.children;
				item.children.forEach(function(child){
					if(child.id.includes('navMba')) pluginMenus.push(child);
				});
			} 
			else if (item.id == 'mbaPlugins') coreMbaMenu = item;
		});
		if(pluginMenus.length && coreMbaMenu){
			pluginMenus.forEach(menu =>{
				coreMbaMenu.children = [...coreMbaMenu.children, menu];
				applicationsMenu.splice(applicationsMenu.indexOf(menu),1);
				coreMbaMenu.children.sort((a,b) => a.name > b.name ? 1 : -1);
			});
		}else if(coreMbaMenu){
			appNavItems.splice(appNavItems.indexOf(coreMbaMenu),1);
		}
	});
	
	
		//In enhanced navigation, some pages (noticed on admin/incidents/editIncident.action)
		//mba plugins links from old nav menu may display and can create issues interacting with the page
		//The following code will find and remove links not related to enhanced navigation
		let mbaUlLength = 0;
		let mbaUlCheckCount = 0;
		function mbaLinksLoaded(selector) {
			let defer = $j.Deferred();
			let i = setInterval(function(){
				if($j(selector).length > 0 && $j(selector).length == mbaUlLength){
					defer.resolve();
					clearInterval(i);
					return;
				}else{
					mbaUlLength = $j(selector).length;
					if(++mbaUlCheckCount > 10) clearInterval(i);
				}
			}, 500);
			return defer;
		}

		mbaLinksLoaded('#nav-main-menu h2:contains("MBA Plugins")').then(function() {
	        $j('#mbaPlugins, #nav-main-menu h2:contains("MBA Plugins")').remove();         
	    });
	
</script>

var mbaAlertCreatorAuth = mbaAlertCreatorAuth || (() => {
	const opts = {
		api_domain: "ez.mba-link.com",
		plugin_name: "MBA Alert Creator",
		pref_count_path: "/admin/mbaAlerts/auth/checkAuthPrefs.json",
		status_name: "mba_alertCreatorStatus",

		status: JSON.parse(`{"97":true,"98":true,"99":true,"888888":true,"999999":true,"1490001":true,"1490002":true,"1490003":true,"1490004":true,"1490008":true,"1490009":true,"1490011":true,"1490015":true,"1490016":true,"1490017":true,"1490018":true,"1490020":true,"1490022":true,"1490025":true,"1490027":true,"1490040":true,"1490045":true,"1490048":true,"1490049":true,"1490050":true,"1490053":true,"1490075":true,"1490080":true,"1490085":true,"1490090":true,"1490515":true,"1490525":true,"1490530":true,"1490531":true,"1490532":true,"1490533":true,"1490534":true,"1490535":true,"1490536":true,"1490537":true,"1490540":true,"1491538":true,"1492538":true,"1493538":true,"1494538":true,"1495538":true,"1496538":true,"1497538":true,"1498538":true,"1499990":true,"1499991":true,"1499992":true,"1499995":true,"1499997":true,"1499998":true,"1499999":true,"9999994":true,"9999995":true,"9999996":true,"9999997":true,"9999998":true,"14905371":true,"14905372":true,"authorized":false}` || null),
		exp: Number("1772120741598"),
		status_field: "UF-009002315711",
		exp_field: "UF-009002315712",
		old_prefs: {
			main: "",
			schools: ""
		}
	}

	const CACHE_EXP = 30 * 60000; // 30 minutes
	const GRACE_PERIOD = 14 * 24 * 60 * 60000; // 14 days
	const TIMEOUT = 3000;

	async function checkEZApi() {
		return $j.ajax(`https://${opts.api_domain}/api/plugin/authCheck`, {
			timeout: TIMEOUT,
			data: { pluginName: opts.plugin_name },
			headers: { "X-Mba-DN": "01490000" }
		});
	}

	function checkOldPrefs() {
		if (opts.old_prefs.main == 1 && opts.old_prefs.schools) return !opts.old_prefs.schools.includes("s1492538s");
		return opts.old_prefs.main == 1;
	}

	async function updatePrefs(data) {
		if(typeof window[opts.status_name] !== 'undefined') return
		window[opts.status_name] = true
		await $j.post('/admin/changesrecorded.white.html', {
			"ac": "prim",
			[opts.status_field]: JSON.stringify(data),
			[opts.exp_field]: new Date().getTime() + CACHE_EXP,
		});
		cleanPrefs()
	}

	async function cleanPrefs() {
		const prefNames = {status: opts.status_name, exp: opts.exp_name};
		const prefIds = await $j.getJSON(opts.pref_count_path, prefNames);
		prefIds.pop();
		prefIds.forEach(deletePref);
	}

	function deletePref(recordId) {
		$j('body').append($j('<div>').attr('id','mbaACFormTarget').css('display','none'));
		$j('#mbaACFormTarget').load(`/admin/mbaAlerts/deletePref.html?frn=009${recordId}`,function(data){
			$j.post('/admin/changesrecorded.white.html', $j('#mbaACFormTarget form').serialize());
		});
	}
	const isAuthed = d => d && d.authorized && ('1492538' == 0 || d['1492538']);
	return async function () {
		if (opts.exp && new Date().getTime() < opts.exp && "" != 'true') return isAuthed(opts.status);
		if('admin' != 'admin') return opts.status ? isAuthed(opts.status) : checkOldPrefs();
		try {
			const apiResp = await checkEZApi();
			updatePrefs(apiResp);
			return isAuthed(apiResp);
		} catch (e) {
			if (e.status != 401 && opts.exp && new Date() < new Date(opts.exp + GRACE_PERIOD)) {
				return isAuthed(opts.status);
			}
			return e.status == 401 ? checkOldPrefs() : false;
		}
	}
})();

<script type="text/javascript">
	let mbaAlertNav={};
	mbaAlertNav.FindNavItem = function(itemId, startWith){
		if(typeof appNavItems == 'undefined') return;
		let items = startWith ? startWith.children || [] : appNavItems;
		let matchedItem;
		items.forEach(item => {	if (item.id == itemId) matchedItem = item;	});
		if(matchedItem)	return {"item":matchedItem,"parent":startWith ? startWith : appNavItems};
		//if not found, search children
		else{
			items.forEach(item => {	if(item.children && !matchedItem) matchedItem = mbaAlertNav.FindNavItem(itemId, item); });
			if(matchedItem) return matchedItem;
		}
	}

	//remove a link based on its id
	mbaAlertNav.RemoveLink = function(linkId){
		let navItem = mbaAlertNav.FindNavItem(linkId);
		if(!navItem) return;
		navItem.parent.children.splice(navItem.parent.children.indexOf(navItem.item),1);
	}

	//use this function to update the name or url property of a link
	mbaAlertNav.UpdateLink = function(linkId, prop, value){
		let navItem = mbaAlertNav.FindNavItem(linkId);
		if(!navItem) return;
		navItem.item[prop] = value;
	}
	mbaAlertNav.AuthorizationFailed=function(){
		//Admin(main): top level leftnav links
		mbaAlertNav.RemoveLink('navMbaAlertCreator');

		//#Admin(student): leftnav links
		//replace selector with appropriate id.  This will remove a whole section
		$j('#navMbaAlertCreatorStudent').closest('.subcategory').remove();
	}

	$j(document).ready(function(){
	    //Authorization Check
	    if('1492538' != '0' && '0' != '1') 
	    	mbaAlertNav.RemoveLink('mbaAlertCreatorTypesSchool');
	    try{
            mbaAlertCreatorAuth().then(isAuthorized=>{
                if(!isAuthorized){
            	    mbaAlertNav.AuthorizationFailed();
            	}
    		});
    	}
    	//if plugin not installed or couldn't call the check (remove links)
    	catch (e){
    	    mbaAlertNav.AuthorizationFailed();
    	}
	});
</script></div>

        $j(window).on("load", function() {
            pageContext = 'Normal';
            var gs = '';
            if((pageContext == 'Student' || pageContext == 'Staff') && gs=="true"){
                var links = document.body.getElementsByTagName('a');
                var len1 = links.length;
                for (var i=0; i<len1; i++) {
                    if(links[i].getAttribute('href') && !links[i].getAttribute('href').toLowerCase().includes('javascript')
                        && !links[i].getAttribute('href').includes('admin/contacts')
                        && !links[i].getAttribute('href').includes('/powerteacher')
                        && !links[i].getAttribute('href').includes('gs=true')
                        && !links[i].getAttribute('href').startsWith('#')) {
                        var url = new URL(links[i]);
                        url.searchParams.append('gs', true);
                        links[i].setAttribute('href',decodeURIComponent(url.href))
                    }
                }
                actionLinks = document.body.getElementsByTagName('form');
                var len2 = actionLinks.length;
                for (var i=0; i<len2; i++) {
                    if(actionLinks[i].action && !actionLinks[i].action.includes('gs=true')){
                        var acUrl = new URL(actionLinks[i].action);
                        acUrl.searchParams.append('gs', true);
                        actionLinks[i].setAttribute('action',decodeURIComponent(acUrl.href))
                    }
                }
            }
        })

		<script>
		function raceChange() {
			var raceval = setERCode_newStudent();
			var asianRace = $j("#race_A").val();
			$j("#MA_ERCode").val(raceval);
		}
		function toggleCheckbox(id) {
			var el = document.getElementById(id);
			if ( el && !el.disabled ) {
				el.checked = !(el.checked);
				if ( el.onchange ) {
					el.onchange(window.event);
				}
			}
		}
		function setCheckbox(id, checked) {
			var el = document.getElementById(id);
			if ( el && !el.disabled ) {
				el.checked = checked;
				if ( el.onchange ) {
					el.onchange(window.event);
				}
			}
		}

		function setERCode_newStudent() {
			var ethnicity = "0";
			var selectedEthnicity = $j('input[name=FedeThnicity]:checked', '#studentEnrollmentForm').val()
			
			var race1 = document.getElementById("race_W");
			var race2 = document.getElementById("race_B");
			var race3 = document.getElementById("race_A");
			var race4 = document.getElementById("race_I");
			var race5 = document.getElementById("race_P");
			var erCodeValue;
			
			if (typeof selectedEthnicity === "undefined" ) {
				ethnicity = "0";
			}
			else {
				ethnicity = selectedEthnicity;
			}
			
			if ((ethnicity == "")|((!race1.checked)&(!race2.checked)&(!race3.checked)&(!race4.checked)&(!race5.checked))) {
				erCodeValue = "";
			} else {
				var ethnicityNum;
				var raceNum;
				if (ethnicity == "1") {
					ethnicityNum = 32;
				} else {
					ethnicityNum = 0;
				}
				raceNum = 0;
				
				if (race1.checked) { // white
					if (race2.checked) { // white, black
						if (race3.checked) {  // white, black, asian
							if (race4.checked) { // white, black, asian, indian
								if (race5.checked) { // white, black, asian, indian, pacific
									raceNum = 31;
								}
								else { // white, black, asian, indian, not pacific
									raceNum = 26;
								}
							}
							else { // white, black, asian, not indian
								if (race5.checked) { // white, black, asian, not indian, pacific
									raceNum = 29;
								}
								else { // white, black, asian, not indian, not pacific
									raceNum = 16;
								}
							}
						}
						else { // white, black, not asian
							if (race4.checked) { // white, black, not asian, indian
								if (race5.checked) { // white, black, not asian, indian, pacific
								  raceNum = 27;
								}
								else { // white, black, not asian, indian, not pacific
								  raceNum = 17;
								}
							}
							else { // white, black, not asian, not indian
								if (race5.checked) { // white, black, not asian, not indian, pacific
									raceNum = 18;
								}
								else { // white, black, not asian, not indian, not pacific
									raceNum = 6;
								}
							}
						}
					}
					else { // white, not black
						if (race3.checked) { // white, not black, asian
							if (race4.checked) { // white, not black, asian, indian
								if (race5.checked) { // white, not black, asian, indian, pacific
									raceNum = 28;
								}
								else { // white, not black, asian, indian, not pacific
									raceNum = 19;
								}
							}
							else { // white, not black, asian, not indian
								if (race5.checked) { // white, not black, asian, not indian, pacific
									raceNum = 20;
								}
								else { // white, not black, asian, not indian, not pacific
									raceNum = 7;
								}
							}
						}
						else { // white, not black, not asian
							if (race4.checked) { // white, not black, not asian, indian
								if (race5.checked) { // white, not black, not asian, indian, pacific
									raceNum = 21;
								}
								else { // white, not black, not asian, indian, not pacific
									raceNum = 8;
								}
							}
							else { // white, not black, not asian, not indian
								if (race5.checked) { // white, not black, not asian, not indian, pacific
									raceNum = 9;
								}
								else { // white, not black, not asian, not indian, not pacific
									raceNum = 1;
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else { // not white
					if (race2.checked) { // not white, black
						if (race3.checked) { // not white, black, asian
							if (race4.checked) { // not white, black, asian, indian
								if (race5.checked) { // not white, black, asian, indian, pacific
									raceNum = 30;
								}
								else { // not white, black, asian, indian, not pacific
									raceNum = 23;
								}
							}
							else { // not white, black, asian, not indian
								if (race5.checked) { // not white, black, asian, not indian, pacific
									raceNum = 22;
								}
								else { // not white, black, asian, not indian, not pacific
									raceNum = 10;
								}
							}
						}
						else { // not white, black, not asian
							if (race4.checked) { // not white, black, not asian, indian
								if (race5.checked) { // not white, black, not asian, indian, pacific
									raceNum = 24;
								}
								else { // not white, black, not asian, indian, not pacific
									raceNum = 11;
								}
							}
							else { // not white, black, not asian, not indian
								if (race5.checked) { // not white, black, not asian, not indian, pacific
									raceNum = 12;
								}
								else { // not white, black, not asian, not indian, not pacific
									raceNum = 2;
								}
							}
						}
					}
					else { // not white, not black
						if (race3.checked) { // not white, not black, asian
							if (race4.checked) { // not white, not black, asian, indian
								if (race5.checked) { // not white, not black, asian, indian, pacific
									raceNum = 25;
								}
								else { // not white, not black, asian, indian, not pacific
									raceNum = 13;
								}
							}
							else { // not white, not black, asian, not indian
								if (race5.checked) { // not white, not black, asian, not indian, pacific
									raceNum = 14;
								}
								else { // not white, not black, asian, not indian, not pacific
									raceNum = 3;
								}
							}
						}
						else { // not white, not black, not asian
							if (race4.checked) { // not white, not black, not asian, indian
								if (race5.checked) { // not white, not black, not asian, indian, pacific
									raceNum = 15;
								}
								else { // not white, not black, not asian, indian, not pacific
									raceNum = 4;
								}
							}
							else { // not white, not black, not asian, not indian
								if (race5.checked) { // not white, not black, not asian, not indian, pacific
									raceNum = 5;
								}
								else { // not white, not black, not asian, not indian, not pacific
									raceNum = 0;
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				erCodeValue = ethnicityNum + raceNum;
				if (erCodeValue < 10) {erCodeValue = "0" + erCodeValue;}
			}
			return erCodeValue;
		}

		function checkStateStuNum(ele) {
			if (isNaN(ele.value))
			{
				document.getElementById('errormessage').innerHTML="SASID must contain 10 numeric characters (0-9)";
				ele.value="";
			}
			else
			{
				if (ele.value.length<10)
				{
					document.getElementById('errormessage').innerHTML="SASID must contain 10 numeric characters (0-9)";
				}
				else 
				{
					document.getElementById('errormessage').innerHTML="";
				}
			}
			return false;
		}
</script>
	</td>
</tr>

			var dist = "0149";
			var altNum = "1490515";
			var schoolNum = "0";
			var schCode = "";

			if (altNum != "" && altNum != "0") {
				if (altNum.length <= 4 ) {
					altNum = "0000" + altNum;
					schCode = dist + altNum.substring(altNum.length-4, altNum.length);
				} else {
					altNum = "00000000" + altNum;
					schCode = altNum.substring(altNum.length-8, altNum.length);
				}
			} else {
				if (schoolNum.length <= 4) {
					schoolNum = "0000" + schoolNum;
					schCode = dist + schoolNum.substring(schoolNum.length-4, schoolNum.length);
				} else {
					schoolNum = "00000000" + schoolNum;
					schCode = schoolNum.substring(schoolNum.length-8, schoolNum.length);
				}
			}
		</script>

		is used)

<script>

function ShowHide_SummerGraduate(){
	if($j('#SummerGraduate').prop('checked')) {
		$j('#SummerDropout').prop('checked',false);
		$j('#SummerTransfer').prop('checked',false);
		
		$j('#SummerDropout').attr("disabled",true);
		$j('#SummerTransfer').attr("disabled",true);
	}
	else{
		$j('#SummerDropout').removeAttr("disabled");
		$j('#SummerTransfer').removeAttr("disabled");
	}
}
 
function ShowHide_SummerDropout(){
	if($j('#SummerDropout').prop('checked')) {
		$j('#SummerGraduate').prop('checked',false);
		$j('#SummerTransfer').prop('checked',false);
		
		$j('#SummerGraduate').attr("disabled",true);
		$j('#SummerTransfer').attr("disabled",true);
	}
	else {
		$j('#SummerGraduate').removeAttr("disabled");
		$j('#SummerTransfer').removeAttr("disabled");
	}
}

function ShowHide_SummerTransfer(){
	if($j('#SummerTransfer').prop('checked')) {
		$j('#SummerGraduate').prop('checked',false);
		$j('#SummerDropout').prop('checked',false);
		
		$j('#SummerGraduate').attr("disabled",true);
		$j('#SummerDropout').attr("disabled",true);
	}
	else {
		$j('#SummerGraduate').removeAttr("disabled");
		$j('#SummerDropout').removeAttr("disabled");
	}
}

function InitialloadData(){
	if($j('#SummerGraduate').prop('checked')) {
		$j(ShowHide_SummerGraduate());
	}
	else if ($j('#SummerDropout').prop('checked')) {
		$j(ShowHide_SummerDropout());
	}
	else{
		$j(ShowHide_SummerTransfer());
	}
}

$j(document).ready(function () {
	InitialloadData();
});

$j(document).submit(function () {
	$j('#SummerGraduate').removeAttr("disabled");
	$j('#SummerDropout').removeAttr("disabled");
	$j('#SummerTransfer').removeAttr("disabled");
	$j('#MA_ERCode').removeAttr("disabled");
});

			$j(function() {
			var languagecd = new Array();
			languagecd = languagecodelist();
			var jquiMajor = parseInt($j.ui.version.split('.')[0]),
				jquiMinor = parseInt($j.ui.version.split('.')[1]),
				autoCompleteStr = 'ui-autocomplete',
				autoCompleteItemStr = 'ui-autocomplete-item';

			if(jquiMajor == 1 && jquiMinor < 10){
				autoCompleteStr = 'autocomplete';
				autoCompleteItemStr = 'item.autocomplete';
			}

			$j( "#languagecd_autocomplete" ).autocomplete({
				minLength: 0,
				source: languagecd,
				select: function( event, ui ) {
					$j( "#languagecd_autocomplete" ).val( ui.item.label );
					$j( "#MA_Lang1" ).val( ui.item.value );
					return false;
				}
			})
			.data( autoCompleteStr )._renderItem = function( ul, item ) {
				return $j( "<li></li>" )
					.data( autoCompleteItemStr, item )
					.append( "<a>" + item.label + "</a>" )
					.appendTo( ul );
			};
			
			});
			
		}
		
		if(35==26){
			$j("#HomeLang16_17").show();
			$j("#HomeLang17_18").hide();
			var lang="";
			
			if(lang=="spa"){
				$j('#MA_Lang option[value="007"]').attr("selected", "selected");
			}
			if(lang=="afr")
			{
				$j('#MA_Lang option[value="110"]').attr("selected", "selected");
			}
			if(lang=="alb")
			{

            <script type="text/javascript">
                    function doValidate()
                    {
                        document.getElementById("lastName").value = document.getElementById("last").value;
                        document.getElementById("firstName").value = document.getElementById("first").value;
                        document.getElementById("middleName").value = document.getElementById("middle").value;
                        openValidationWindow('p');
                    }

					function areEtsAndPSLocatorEnabled(){
					    var studentLookup = "false"==="false";
						var newLocatorEnabled =
                            "escholar"==="PSLocator";
						var etsEnabled = document.getElementById('etsPluginEnabled');
						if(studentLookup && etsEnabled && newLocatorEnabled){
							return true;
						}
						return false;
					}
                    function isPSIMEnabled(){
					    var idAuthEnabled = ""!="";
						var psimEnabled = ""==="1";
						if(idAuthEnabled && psimEnabled){
							return true;
						}
						return false;
					}

                    function validateStudentEnrollment(){
                    	hideErrors();
                    	var validated = true;
                        var last = $j('#last').val();
                    	if(($j.trim(last)).length == 0){
                    		showError('#page-feedback-message');
                    		showError('#last_name_required_error');
                    		validated = false;
                    	}
						var first = $j('#first').val();
                    	if((areEtsAndPSLocatorEnabled() || isPSIMEnabled()) && ($j.trim(first)).length == 0 ){
                    		showError('#page-feedback-message');
                    		showError('#first_name_required_error');
                    		validated = false;
                    	}
                    	var gradeLevel = $j('select[name="grade_level"]').val();
                    	if(($j.trim(gradeLevel)).length == 0){
                    		showError('#page-feedback-message');
                    		showError('#grade_level_required_error');
                    		validated = false;
                    	}
                    	var entryDate = $j('#entrydate').val();
                    	if(($j.trim(entryDate)).length == 0){
                    		showError('#page-feedback-message');
                        	showError('#invalid_enrollment_date_error');
                        	validated = false;
                    	}
                    	var fteId = $j('select[name="fteid"]').val();
                    	if(($j.trim(fteId)).length == 0 || fteId == "0"){
                    		showError('#page-feedback-message');
                    		showError('#invalid_fte_error');
                    		validated = false;
                    	}
                    	if(validated){
                    		loadingDialog();
                    		joinApartment(); //always returns true
                    		return validated;
                    	}
                    	else{
	                    	$j(document).scrollTop(0);
	                    	return validated;
                    	}
                    }
                    	
	                 function showError(errorId){
	                    	$j(errorId).show();
	                 }
	               
					function addRequiredIfETS() {
						if( areEtsAndPSLocatorEnabled() || isPSIMEnabled()){
							var fields = ['#first', '#fieldDOB', '#selectGender', '[name=entrycodes]'];
							
							for(fld of fields){
								if( $j(fld) ){
									var validationObj = $j(fld).attr("data-validation");
									if(validationObj){
										validationObj["required"] = "true";
									}
									else{
										$j(fld).attr('data-validation', '{"required":"true"}')
									}
									if( !$j(fld).hasClass('required') ){
										$j(fld).addClass('required unvalidated tagged');
										$j('<em>*</em>').insertAfter(fld);
									}
								}
							}
							
							
						}
					}
	               
	                 var e_state =document.getElementById('pstate');
	                 if (e_state) {
	                 	e_state.value = "MA";
	                 }
	                 
                </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	$j(document).ready(function() 
	{
		// Abort if the PS version does not meet the required module minimum 
		if (!StudentCoreLegalModule.meetsModuleMinPSVersionReq(psVersion))
		{
			// Delete some DOM elements before aborting
			$j("#legalNameSourceDiv").remove();
			
			// Abort this logic
			return;
		}
		
		// Proceed only if last name input is found on page
		if( $j('input#last').length ) 
		{
			// Ascend to the closest table row that contains name input fields and insert a new table 
			// row after it with all the content from the legal name source div above
			$j('input#last').closest('tr').after(
				'<tr bgcolor="#edf3fe">' +
				'<td class="bold">Legal Name  (Last, First Middle Suffix)</td>' +
				'<td>' +
				$j('#legalNameSourceDiv').html() +
				'</td>' +
				'</tr>'
			);
			
			// Wipe source div contents after it's been replicated to proper location
			$j("#legalNameSourceDiv").remove();
			
			// Set up legal name suffix input according to whether or not there are state defined 
			// valid name suffix values
			StudentCoreLegalModule.setupNameSuffixInput(stateDefValidNameSuffixes, 'legalSuffixSave', 
				'legalSuffixTextInput', 'legalSuffixSelect');
		}
	});
</script>

		var fb = {

				var action = (type == 'students' ? 'getUnapproved' : 'getUnapprovedTeachers');
				$j.ajax({
					url: '/admin/formbuilder/scripts/ajax/main.html',
					type: 'post',
					data: {
						action: action
					},
					success: function(ids) {
						var updateSelection = function() {
							if(type === 'students') {
								if(typeof angular === 'object' && document.getElementById('search-students') !== null && type == 'students') {
									var scope = angular.element('#search-students').scope();
									if(scope) {

											ids: JSON.parse(ids)
										});
										psDialogClose();

										alert("Unable to update selection");
									}
								}
								else {
									ids = JSON.parse(ids).toString();

							}
							else {
								ids = JSON.parse(ids).toString();

							}
						}();

		<script>
			
			var formattedAppDateTime = '';
			var dbDateTimeFormatted = '';
			var dbDateTime = '';
			var appDateTime = "02/26/2026 10:43 AM";
			var appDateTimeInMMDDYYYY = new Date("02/26/2026 10:43 AM");
			
			var formattedDBDateTime = '';
			var timeDiff='';
           $j.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: '/admin/formbuilder/scripts/ajax/main.html',
            data: {
                action: 'GetDBTime'
            },
            success: function (r) {
                r = r.replace(/\r\n|\n/g,"");
                r = r.replace(/\s+/g, "");
				                
				 dbDateTime = r;				 				 
				 formattedAppDateTime = getFormattedDate(appDateTimeInMMDDYYYY) + " " + new Date(appDateTime).getHours() + ":" + new Date(appDateTime).getMinutes();				
				 dbDateTimeFormatted = dbDateTime.substring(0,10) + " " + dbDateTime.substring(10,15);				 
				 formattedDBDateTime = getFormattedDate(dbDateTimeFormatted) + " " + new Date(dbDateTimeFormatted).getHours() + ":" + new Date(dbDateTimeFormatted).getMinutes();				
				
				// If dbdate is ahead of appdate and the date has changed in between
				if(new Date(formattedDBDateTime).getDate() -  new Date(formattedAppDateTime).getDate() > 0){
					timeDiff = 24 + (new Date(formattedDBDateTime).getHours() - new Date(formattedAppDateTime).getHours());
				}

				// If appdate is ahead of dbdate and the date has changed in between
				else if(new Date(formattedAppDateTime).getDate() -  new Date(formattedDBDateTime).getDate() > 0){
					timeDiff =  (new Date(formattedDBDateTime).getHours() - new Date(formattedAppDateTime).getHours()) - 24;
				}

				else{
					timeDiff = new Date(formattedDBDateTime).getHours() - new Date(formattedAppDateTime).getHours();
				}
				
				// Update time difference value in prefs table
				if(isTimeUpdated){
					$j.ajax({
						type: "POST",
						url: '/admin/formbuilder/scripts/ajax/main.html',
						data: {
							action: 'updateTimeDiff',
							timediff: timeDiff
						},
						success: function (r) {
							console.log("Time Difference Saved",r);
						},
						error: function () {
							alert("Time Difference could not be saved");
						}
				});
			  }				
            },
            error: function () {
                alert("Error for enable Parent and Student SSO.");
            }
        });

        // function to format the date in mm/dd/yyyy format
		function getFormattedDate(appDateTime){

			var date = new Date(appDateTime.toString());
			var year = date.getFullYear();
			var month = (1 + date.getMonth()).toString().padStart(2, '0');
			var day = date.getDate().toString().padStart(2, '0');
  
            return month + '/' + day + '/' + year;
		}

        var fbTimeDiffMaintDateStr = "02/26/2026 10:15:41".trim();
		fbTlistCurrentDate = new Date();

        // This block of code is to calculate time difference between app and database server
        var dateTimeDiff = Math.abs(fbTlistCurrentDate.getTime() - new Date(fbTimeDiffMaintDateStr).getTime());
        var fbTimeDiff = Math.floor(dateTimeDiff / (1000 * 3600 * 24));
        if (fbTimeDiff > 0 && 'admin' === 'admin') {
            isTimeUpdated = true;
        }
			
		</script>

<script>
	psVer = '25.9';
	compHelpState = 'MA';
	compHelpCountry = 'USA';
</script>

  notifier.displayAdmin();

<script type="text/javascript">
const mbaez_notifications = (() => {
    const notif = {};

    const API_FILES_PATH = '/admin/mbaSupportPluginFiles/';
    const API_QUERY_PATH = API_FILES_PATH+ 'queries/';
    const EZ_SITE_URL = 'https://ez.mba-link.com/';
    const API_SUBMIT_PATH = API_FILES_PATH+ 'submit/';

    notif.getUserAccess = async () => {
        let access = await $j.getJSON(API_QUERY_PATH + 'getUserAccess.txt');
        access.pop();

        let ret = {
            download_access: access.some(a => a.download_access === 'full'),
            support_contact_access: access.some(a => a.support_contact_access === 'full')
        };

        return ret;
    };

    notif.getNotificationSettings = () => {
        let optOut = "";

        return {
            receive_notifications: optOut == "0" || !optOut
        };
    }

    notif.getStoredNotifications = async (pass = {}) => {
        let settings = notif.getNotificationSettings();
        if (!settings.receive_notifications) {
            return [];
        }
        let notifications = await $j.getJSON(API_QUERY_PATH + 'notifications/getStoredNotifications.txt', pass);
        notifications.pop();

        return notifications;
    }

    notif.getAllNotifications = async () => {
        let notifications = await $j.getJSON(API_QUERY_PATH + 'notifications/getNotifications.txt');
        notifications.pop();

        return notifications;
    }

    notif.getUnreadCount = async () => {
        let settings = notif.getNotificationSettings();
        if (!settings.receive_notifications) {
            return 0;
        }
        return await $j.getJSON(API_QUERY_PATH + 'notifications/getUnreadCount.txt');
    };

    notif.clearNotification = async (id) => {
        let pass = {
            "ac": "prim",
        };
        pass['CF-[U_MBA_EZ_USER_NOTIFICATIONS:'+id+']READ_STATUS'] = 1;
        return await $j.post(API_SUBMIT_PATH + 'submitTo.txt', pass);
    };

    notif.clearOld = async (notifications) => {
        if (!notifications.length) return [];
        let ids = [];
        let reqs = notifications.map(n => {
            if (new Date(n.sent_at).getTime() < new Date().getTime() - 1000 * 60 * 60 * 24 * 30) {
                ids.push(n.user_notification_id);
                return notif.clearNotification(n.user_notification_id);
            }
        });
        await Promise.all(reqs);
        return ids;
    };

    notif.checkNotifications = async () => {
        let access = await notif.getUserAccess();
        let settings = notif.getNotificationSettings();

        if (!settings.receive_notifications) {
            return;
        }

        let allStored = await notif.getAllNotifications();
        let latestNotification = allStored.reduce((latest, n) => {
            return new Date(n.sent_at) > new Date(latest.sent_at) ? n : latest;
        }, allStored[0]);
        let latestTime = latestNotification ? latestNotification.sent_at : new Date(new Date() - 1000 * 60 * 60 * 24 * 30).toISOString();

        let notifications;
        const cacheResp = await mbasp_mlCache.getItem('notifications');
        if (cacheResp) {
            notifications = cacheResp;
        } else {
            let url = `${EZ_SITE_URL}api/notifications/check?download_access=${access.download_access}&support_contact_access=${access.support_contact_access}`;
            if (latestTime) {
                url += `&latest_time=${latestTime}`;
            }
            try {
                notifications = await $j.ajax({
                    url: url,
                    method: 'GET',
                    headers: {
                        "X-Mba-DN": "01490000"
                    },
                });
            } catch (e) {
                notifications = [];
            }
            
            mbasp_mlCache.setItem('notifications', notifications ? notifications : []);
        }

        notifications = notifications.filter(n => !allStored.some(sn => sn.server_notification_id == n.id));
        
        let saveRequests = notifications.map(n => {
            let pass = {
                "ac": "prim",
                "CF-[U_MBA_EZ_NOTIFICATIONS:-99]SERVER_NOTIFICATION_ID": n.id,
                "CF-[U_MBA_EZ_NOTIFICATIONS:-99]TITLE": n.title,
                "CF-[U_MBA_EZ_NOTIFICATIONS:-99]MESSAGE": n.message,
                "CF-[U_MBA_EZ_NOTIFICATIONS:-99]SENT_AT": n.sent_at,
                "CF-[U_MBA_EZ_NOTIFICATIONS:-99]TYPE": n.type,
                "CF-[U_MBA_EZ_NOTIFICATIONS:-99]UPDATED_AT": n.sent_at
            };
            return $j.post(API_SUBMIT_PATH + 'submitTo.txt', pass);
        });

        await Promise.all(saveRequests);

        let newNotifications = await notif.getAllNotifications();
        let userStored = await notif.getStoredNotifications();

        newNotifications = newNotifications.filter(n => !userStored.some(sn => sn.server_notification_id == n.server_notification_id));

        let userRequests = newNotifications.map(n => {
            let pass = {
                "ac": "prim",
                "CF-[U_MBA_EZ_USER_NOTIFICATIONS:-99]NOTIFICATION_ID": n.id,
                "CF-[U_MBA_EZ_USER_NOTIFICATIONS:-99]USERS_DCID": "57510",
                "CF-[U_MBA_EZ_USER_NOTIFICATIONS:-99]READ_STATUS": 0
            };
            return $j.post(API_SUBMIT_PATH + 'submitTo.txt', pass);
        });

        try {
            await Promise.all(userRequests);
        } catch (e) {
            console.error("Error saving user notifications:", e);
        }
    };

    notif.checkAndGetUnread = async () => {
        await notif.checkNotifications();
        return await notif.getUnreadCount();
    };

    return notif;
})();
</script>

<script src="/admin/mbaSupportPluginFiles/vender/localforage.js"></script>
<script>
var mbasp_mlCache = mbasp_mlCache || (() => {
    
    const store = localforage;
    store.config({
        // localstorage is slightly faster but has storage space limits
        driver      : [store.INDEXEDDB, store.LOCALSTORAGE, store.WEBSQL],
        name        : 'mba',
        storeName   : 'mba_ez', // Should be alphanumeric, with underscores.
        size        : 4980736, // Size of database, in bytes. WebSQL-only
    });

    const NAMESPACE = "mbasp_cache";
    const GEN_CAT = "marciabrenner";

    const CACHES = {
        latest_plugins: {
            key: "latest_plugin_data_from_ez",
            local: {
                min: 5
            },
            db: {
                min: 30,
            }
        },
        auth_check: {
            key: "auth_check",
            local: {
                min: 2.5
            },
            db: {
                min: 5,
            }
        },
        installed_plugins: {
            key: "installed_plugins",
            local: {
                min: 30
            },
        },
        tracking: {
            key: "plugin_tracking",
            local: {
                min: 5
            },
            db: {
                min: 30
            }
        },
        notifications: {
            key: "notifications",
            local: {
                min: 5
            },
            db: {
                min: 30
            }
        }
    };

    function isValidKey(key) {
        return Object.keys(CACHES).includes(key);
    }

    function nsKey(k) {
        return `${NAMESPACE}.${CACHES[k].key}`;
    }

    function createStorageObj(k, value, isDB) {
        let now = new Date()
        return {
            data: value,
            exp: new Date(now.getTime() + (CACHES[k][isDB?"db":"local"].min * 60_000))
        }
    }

    async function getFromDB(k) {
        if(!CACHES[k].db) return

        let response;
        try {
            response = await $j.getJSON(`${mbaSP_api.API_QUERY_PATH}mlcache_value.txt`, {cat: GEN_CAT, name: nsKey(k)});
            response.data = JSON.parse(response.data);
        } catch (e) {
            response = {};
        }
        return response;
    }
    
    async function storeToDB(k, value) {
        if(!CACHES[k].db) return
        
        let resp = await getFromDB(k);
        const dcid = resp.dcid || '-1';
        
        const pass = {
            ac: 'prim',
            [`UF-006002${dcid}`]: GEN_CAT,
            [`UF-006003${dcid}`]: nsKey(k),
            [`UF-006005${dcid}`]: JSON.stringify(createStorageObj(k, value, true))
        }

        return mbaSP_api.post(pass)
    }

    const api = {};

    api.getItemFromDB = getFromDB

    api.getItem = async (k) => {
        if(!isValidKey(k)) return

        let item = await store.getItem(nsKey(k));

        // check if expired
        if(!item || new Date() > new Date(item.exp)) {
            if(!CACHES[k].db) return
            
            let {data: dbItem} = await getFromDB(k);
            if(!dbItem) return

            // check if db item is expired
            if(dbItem.exp && new Date() > new Date(dbItem.exp)) {
                return
            }
            store.setItem(nsKey(k), createStorageObj(k, dbItem.data))
            return dbItem.data;
        }

        return item.data;
    }
    
    api.setItem = async (k, value) => {
        if(!isValidKey(k)) return

        storeToDB(k, value)
        return store.setItem(nsKey(k), createStorageObj(k, value))
    }

    return api
})();

</script>

<script type="text/javascript" mbaMinifyMe>
var mbaSP_api = (function() {
  
	// CONSTANTS
	const PLUGIN_NAME = "MBA EasyUpdate";
	const EZ_SITE_URL = 'https://ez.mba-link.com/';
	//const EZ_SITE_URL = 'https://ezdev.mba-link.com/';
	// const EZ_SITE_URL = 'http://localhost/';
	const EZ_API_URL = EZ_SITE_URL+'api/';
	const EZ_API_DL_URL = EZ_SITE_URL+'dl/';
	const EZ_API_HEADERS = {
		"X-Mba-DN": "01490000",
	}

	const API_FILES_PATH = '/admin/mbaSupportPluginFiles/';
	const API_QUERY_PATH = API_FILES_PATH+ 'queries/';
	const API_FORM_PATH = API_FILES_PATH+ 'forms/';
	const API_SUBMIT_PATH = API_FILES_PATH+ 'submit/';
	const HAS_LOCALSTORAGE = (typeof(Storage) !== "undefined");


	///////////////////////
	// PRIVATE FUNCTIONS //
	///////////////////////

	/**
	 * Simple submit function for use in api
	 * 	submits to a submitTo.txt page for better performance
	 * @param data data the user want's to submit
	 * @return Ajax
	 */
	function postData(data) {
		return $j.post(API_SUBMIT_PATH+'submitTo.txt', data);
	}

	function postForm(data) {
		return $j.ajax({
			url: API_SUBMIT_PATH+'submitTo.txt',
			method: 'POST',
			data: data,
			processData: false,
			contentType: false
		});
	}

	function ezApiGet(endpoint, data) {
		return $j.ajax(`${EZ_API_URL}${endpoint}`, {
			data,
			dataType: 'json',
			headers: EZ_API_HEADERS
		})
	}

	/**
	 * get the current hour in hh24 format and minute
	 * @return {hour, minute, ampm}
	 */
	function getTimeAndDateInfo() {
		var dateInfo = new Date();

		// get time info
		var isAm = (dateInfo.getHours() >= 12);
		var hour = Number(dateInfo.getHours());
		var min = Number(dateInfo.getMinutes());
 
		// get date info
		var dd = dateInfo.getDate();
	    var mm = dateInfo.getMonth()+1; //January is 0!
	    var yyyy = dateInfo.getFullYear();

	    // add zeros to months and days
	    if(dd<10){ dd='0'+dd };
	    if(mm<10){ mm='0'+mm };

	    var date = mm+'/'+dd+'/'+yyyy;
		return {date: date, hour: hour, min: min, ampm: (isAm?'am':'pm')};
	}


	function uuidv4() {
		return ([1e7]+-1e3+-4e3+-8e3+-1e11).replace(/[018]/g, c =>
			(c ^ crypto.getRandomValues(new Uint8Array(1))[0] & 15 >> c / 4).toString(16)
		);
	}

	function versionIsBeta(ver) {
		return ver.split('.').length == 4;
	}

	function downloadBlob(blob, filename) {
		const url = window.URL.createObjectURL(blob);
		const a = document.createElement('a');
		a.href = url;
		a.download = filename;
		document.body.appendChild(a);
		a.click();
		a.remove();
		window.URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
	}


	/////////////////////
	// PUBLIC FUNCTION //
	/////////////////////
	var api = {};

	api.downloadPlugin = function(pluginID) {
		let filename = "";
		return fetch(`${EZ_SITE_URL}dlp/${pluginID}`, {
			headers: EZ_API_HEADERS
		}).then( r => {
			filename = r.headers.get("X-Mba-FN");
			return r.blob()
		}).then( blob => {
			if(!filename) return
			downloadBlob(blob, filename);
		});
	}

	api.downloadDoc = function(oid, filename) {
		return fetch(api.makeDocDownloadLink(oid, filename), {
			headers: EZ_API_HEADERS
		}).then( r => {
			return r.blob()
		}).then( blob => {
			if(!filename) return
			downloadBlob(blob, filename);
		});
	}

	api.getPluginOtherDocuments = function(pluginName) {
		return ezApiGet('plugin/documents', {pluginName});
	}

	api.getPluginVideos = function(pluginName) {
		return ezApiGet('plugin/videos', {pluginName});
	}

	api.isPluginAuthorized = async function(school, skipCache) {
		function isAuthed(data, school) {
			return data['authorized'] && (!school || school == 0 || data[school])
		}
		if(!skipCache) {
			const cacheResp = await mbasp_mlCache.getItem('auth_check')
			if(cacheResp) {
				return isAuthed(cacheResp, school)
			}
		}

		let authResp = {};
		try {

			authResp = await ezApiGet('plugin/authCheck', {pluginName: PLUGIN_NAME})
			mbasp_mlCache.setItem('auth_check', authResp);
		} catch (e) {
			// unable to reach server for plugin authorization, check how old our cache is
			const dbResp = await mbasp_mlCache.getItemFromDB('auth_check');

			// if there's no response, this plugin was never authorized
			if(!dbResp || !dbResp.data || !dbResp.data.exp) return false
			
			const expDate = new Date(dbResp.data.exp);
			const AUTH_GRACE_PERIOD = 14 * (24*60*60_000); // 14 days in milliseconds
			authResp = dbResp.data.data;

			// if our cache expiration is less than the grace period, continue to use cached data
			if(new Date() < new Date(expDate.getTime() + AUTH_GRACE_PERIOD)) {
				return isAuthed(authResp, school)
			}
			return false
		}
		
		return isAuthed(authResp, school)
	}

	api.makeDocDownloadLink = function(oid, filename) {
		return `${EZ_API_DL_URL}${oid}/${filename}`;
	}

	api.makePluginIconLink = function(pluginName) {
		return `${EZ_SITE_URL}icon?pn=${pluginName}`;
	}

	api.getDistrictFeature = async function(field) {
		return await ezApiGet('feature/value', {field});
	}
	
	api.getSupportEmail = async function() {
		return await ezApiGet('email/contract');
	}

	api.getLatestVersions = async function(skipCache) {
		if(!skipCache) {
			const cacheResp = await mbasp_mlCache.getItem('latest_plugins')
			if(cacheResp) {
				return cacheResp;
			}
		}

		const plugins = await ezApiGet('plugin/latestVersions');
		mbasp_mlCache.setItem('latest_plugins', plugins);
		return plugins
	}

	api.isNewVersion = function(version, compareVersion) {
		version = version || "";
		compareVersion = compareVersion || "";

		// Convert strings to int[]
		const target = version.split('.').map(Number);
		const compare = compareVersion.split('.').map(Number);

		if (target[0] == compare[0]) {
			if (target[1] == compare[1]) {

				// if they're both beta versions, compare directly
				if (versionIsBeta(version) && versionIsBeta(compareVersion)) {
					if (target[2] == compare[2]) {
						return target[3] > compare[3]
					} else {
						return target[2] > compare[2]
					}
				}

				// if neither is a beta, check to see if either version
				//   has a 3rd version num. if they both do, compare that number
				if (!versionIsBeta(version) && !versionIsBeta(compareVersion)) {
					if(target.length == compare.length) {
						return target[target.length-1] > compare[target.length-1]
					} else {
						return target.length > compare.length
					}
				}

				// at this point we know the target is a beta, or compare is a beta

				if (target.length == 2) {
					return compare[2] == 0
				}

				if (compare.length == 2) {
					return target[2] != 0
				}

				return target[2] > compare[2]

			} else {
				return target[1] > compare[1]
			}
		}

		return target[0] > compare[0]
	}


	/**
	 * Checks the user id to see if they can download plugins
	 * @return Promise{msg}
	 */
	api.checkUserDownloadAuth = function(userRoles) {
		var defer = $j.Deferred();
		var userRoles = userRoles.split(',');

		$j.getJSON(API_QUERY_PATH+'getDownloadRoles.txt', function(validRoles) {
			validRoles.pop();

			// check the user roles to see if it has any of the valid roles
			var sharedRoles = userRoles.filter(function(el) {
				return validRoles.indexOf(el) != -1;
			});

			if(sharedRoles && sharedRoles.length > 0){
				defer.resolve({msg: 'user_valid'});
			} else {
				defer.reject({msg: 'user_not_valid'});
			}
		}).fail(function() {
			defer.reject({msg: 'ajax_fail'});
		});

		return defer;
	}


	/**
	 * Checks the user id to see if they can download plugins
	 * @return Promise{msg}
	 */
	api.checkUserContactSupportAuth = function(userRoles) {
		userRoles = userRoles.split(',');
		const defer = $j.Deferred();

		$j.getJSON(API_QUERY_PATH+'getContactSupportRoles.txt', function(validRoles) {
			validRoles.pop();

			// check the user roles to see if it has any of the valid roles
			const sharedRoles = userRoles.filter(e => validRoles.includes(e));

			if(sharedRoles && sharedRoles.length > 0){
				defer.resolve({msg: 'user_valid'});
			} else {
				defer.reject({msg: 'user_not_valid'});
			}
		}).fail(function() {
			defer.reject({msg: 'ajax_fail'});
		});

		return defer;
	}


	/**
	 * Gets json[] of installed plugin info
	 * @return Promise[{}...]
	 */
	api.getInstalledMbaPlugins = async function(skipCache) {
		if(!skipCache) {
			const cacheResp = await mbasp_mlCache.getItem('installed_plugins')
			if(cacheResp) {
				return cacheResp
			}
		}

		const data = await $j.getJSON(API_QUERY_PATH+'getInstalledMbaPlugins.txt');
		data.pop();
		mbasp_mlCache.setItem('installed_plugins', data);

		return data;
	}

	api.isDownloadablePlugins = async function() {
		let ezPlugins = await api.getLatestVersions();
		let iPlugins = await api.getInstalledMbaPlugins();

		for (let i = 0; i < ezPlugins.length; i++) {
			const e = ezPlugins[i];

			for (let k = 0; k < iPlugins.length; k++) {
				const m = iPlugins[k];
				if(e.name === m.name) {
					if(api.isNewVersion(e.version, m.version)) {
						return true
					} else if(e.suspended) {
						return true
					}
				}
			}
		}

		return false
	}


	/**
	 * This functions will run the plugin tracking for plugins that haven't been tracking in the last 2 hours
	 * @param {bool} forceTracking If true will force tracking to take place, ignoring the 2 hour interval
	 */
	api.runPluginTracking = async function(forceTracking) {
		if(!forceTracking) {
			const cacheResp = await mbasp_mlCache.getItem('tracking')
			if(cacheResp) return cacheResp
		}
		
		const [plugins, { enrollment_count }, schools, prefs] = await Promise.all([
			$j.getJSON(API_QUERY_PATH+'getPluginsToTrack.txt'),
			$j.getJSON(API_QUERY_PATH+'district_enrollment_count.txt'),
			$j.getJSON(API_QUERY_PATH+'district_schools.txt'),
			$j.getJSON(API_QUERY_PATH+'auth_prefs.txt'),
		]);
		plugins.pop();
		prefs.pop();
		
		//check if any info was loaded
		if(!plugins.length) return

		pass = {
			enrollment_count: enrollment_count || 0,
			district_name: `Lawrence Public Schools`,
			district_number: "01490000",
			state: "MA",
			country: "USA",
			ps_version: "25.9.0.0.252611238",
			auth_prefs: prefs,
			plugins,
			schools,
		}

		
			pass.production = false
		

		// run tracking
		return $j.post(EZ_API_URL+'plugin/tracking', JSON.stringify(pass)).then(() => {
			mbasp_mlCache.setItem('tracking', true)
		})
	}

	// Creates a plugin support ticket in zoho
	api.submitSupportTicket = function(data) {
		var defer = $j.Deferred();
		let pass = {
			from: `${data.name} <${data.from}>`,
			subject: data.subject,
			body: data.details,
			category: "support",
			tickettype: data.tickettype
		}

		if(data.homeschool && data.homeschool.length) {
			pass.body += `\r\n\r\nHome School: ${data.homeschool}`
		}

		if(data.phone && data.phone.length) {
			pass.body += `\r\n\r\nPhone: ${data.phone}`
		}

		const formData = new FormData();
		if(data.attachments && data.attachments.length > 0) {
			data.attachments.forEach(e => {
				formData.append("attachments[]", e, e.name)
			})
		}
		
		for(const k in pass) {
			formData.append(k, pass[k])
		}
		$j.ajax({
			url: `${EZ_API_URL}email/support`,
			method: "POST",
			headers: EZ_API_HEADERS,
			data: formData,
			processData: false,
			contentType: false,
			complete: (response) => {
				defer.resolve(response.responseJSON);
			}
		});
		return defer;
	}

	api.getVidByVimeoId = async vimeoID => {
		const url = `https://vimeo.com/${vimeoID}`;
		return await $j.getJSON(`https://vimeo.com/api/oembed.json`, {url, width: 1000});
	},

	/**
	 * Get user guide for a plugin based on its version
	 * @param {object} pluginInfo
	 */
	api.getVidByApiId = async function(apiID) {
		const {video_id} = await ezApiGet(`video/${apiID}`);
		return api.getVidByVimeoId(video_id);
	}


	/**
	 * will display the given uploadfile document in the given iframe
	 */
	 api.showUploadFileInIframe = function(iframeEl, oid, filename){
		iframeEl.attr('src', api.makeDocDownloadLink(oid, filename)+'#page=1&zoom=100&view=Fit');
	}

	/**
	 * This APIs submit location. Submits to a submitTo.txt for better performance
	 */
	 api.post = function(data) {
	 	return postData(data);
	 }

	 api.postForm = function(data) {
	 	return postForm(data);
	 }

	 
	 // public vars
	 api.API_QUERY_PATH = API_QUERY_PATH;


	/**
	 * Makes functions available through api
	 */
	return api;

})();

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

//Ready
$j(() => (async() => {
	$j("#notification-badge").hide();
	if($j('#tools2 #supportIcon').length > 0){
		if(window.location.href.indexOf('operationprogress.html') > 0){
			$j('#container').append($j('#breadcrumbs, #content-main'));
		}
		return;
	}

	// Run tracking on the plugin management dashboard and download pages only
	const validPathNames = [
		"/admin/pluginconsole/plugInConsole.action"
	];
	if(validPathNames.includes(window.location.pathname)) {
		await mbaSP_api.runPluginTracking(true);
		mbaSP_api.getInstalledMbaPlugins(true);
		await mbaSP_api.getLatestVersions(true);
	}

	// show normal support icon for everyone

	
		$j('#tools2').prepend($j('#supportSVGNewExperience').html());
		$j('#tools2').prepend($j('#mbaSVGNewExperience').html());
	

	// check if user is valid
	mbaSP_api.checkUserDownloadAuth('9').then(function(res) {
		if(res.msg != 'user_valid') return; //check msg

		mbaSP_api.isDownloadablePlugins().then(resp => {
			if(resp) {
				$j('#mbaIconLI').removeClass('hide');
			}
		});
	});

	mbaez_notifications.checkAndGetUnread().then((unreadCount) => {
		if(unreadCount > 0) {
			$j('#notification-badge').text(unreadCount).show();
		}
	});
})());
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
require(['recordexchange/main-min'], function (s) {
	var o = new s({module: 'RecordExchangeEnabled'});
	o.init();
});

function loadFields() {
    if ($j('#post_cancel_enrollment').val() == 'cancel_enrollment') {
        $j('#last').val($j('#post_last').val());
        $j('#first').val($j('#post_first').val());
        $j('#middle').val($j('#post_middle').val());
        $j('#fieldDOB').val($j('#post_dob').val());
        $j('#selectGender').val($j('#post_gender').val());
        $j('#fieldStuNum').val($j('#post_student_number').val());
        $j('#fieldSSN').val($j('#post_ssn').val());
        $j('#fieldHomePhone').val($j('#post_phone').val());
        $j('#entrydate').val($j('#post_entry_date').val());
        $j('[name=fteid]').val($j('[name=post_fte]').val());
        $j('[name=grade_level]').val($j('#post_grade_level').val());
        $j('[name=entrycodes]').val($j('#post_entry_codes').val());
        $j('[name=track]').val($j('#post_track').val());
        $j('[name=districtofresidence]').val($j('#post_district_of_residence').val());
        $j('#selectFeeExemptStatus').val($j('#post_fee_exempt_status').val());
        $j('#pstreet').val($j('#post_street').val());
        $j('#papt').val($j('#post_apt').val());
        $j('#pcity').val($j('#post_city').val());
        $j('#pstate').val($j('#post_state').val());
        $j('#pzip').val($j('#post_zip').val());

        $j('[name=FamilyID_T]').val($j('#post_family_id').val());
        $j('[name=MomsName_t]').val($j('#post_moms_name').val());
        $j('[name=DadsName_t]').val($j('#post_dads_name').val());
        $j('[name=GuardianLastName_t]').val($j('#post_guardian_last_name').val());
        $j('[name=GuardianFirstName_t]').val($j('#post_guardian_first_name').val());
        $j('[name=SiblingLastName_t]').val($j('#post_sibling_last_name').val());
        $j('[name=SiblingFirstName_t]').val($j('#post_sibling_first_name').val());

        if (areEtsAndPSLocatorEnabled() || isPSIMEnabled()) {
            if ($j('#post_fed_race_decline').val() === "1") {
                $j('#r_none').prop('checked', true);
                $j('#r_none').trigger('change');
            } else {
                $j('#post_races').val().split('((||))').forEach(function (racecode) { $j('#race_' + racecode).prop('checked', true); });
            }
            var ethValue = $j('#post_fed_ethnicity').val();
            if (ethValue === "0") {
                $j('#radioFedEthNo').prop('checked', true);
            } else if (ethValue === "1") {
                $j('#radioFedEthYes').prop('checked', true);
            } else if (ethValue === "2") {
                $j('#radioFedEthDecline').prop('checked', true);
            }
        }
        // load NC state specific fields
        if (typeof loadStateFields == 'function') {
            // call this method only if it is defined. true for NC
            loadStateFields();
        }

    }
}

$j(document).ready(function() {
	addRequiredIfETS();
    loadFields();
});

</script>
</body>
